[2;36m                    [0m         [39m# Evaluation Report[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Summary[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mA heap-buffer-overflow was detected by AddressSanitizer in the HTML parsing [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcomponent of libxml2. The overflow occurs during comment parsing in the function [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`htmlSecureComment` when copying data into a buffer allocated by the fuzzer [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mharness. This issue was surfaced by a libFuzzer run on the HTML parser with a [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mspecially crafted input.[0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Description[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mIssue Details  [0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The fuzzer invoked `LLVMFuzzerTestOneInput` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mfuzz/html.[0m[1;92mc:49[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, which calls into [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`htmlCtxtParseDocument`.  [0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- During parsing, `htmlSecureComment` in `HTMLparser.c` allocates a buffer via [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`xmlFuzzMalloc` and then performs a `memcpy` that writes [0m[1;36m105[0m[39m bytes beyond the end [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mof a [0m[1;36m501[0m[39m-byte region, immediately triggering a heap-buffer-overflow.  [0m              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- AddressSanitizer reports the overflow at `htmlSecureComment` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mHTMLparser.[0m[1;92mc:3591[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m,[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mon the instruction `__asan_memcpy`, indicating a multi-byte write past the [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mallocated heap buffer.  [0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mVulnerability Type  [0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Memory corruption: heap-buffer-overflow.  [0m                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mKey Observations  [0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The overflow address `[0m[1;36m0x515000000775[0m[39m` is exactly at the byte after the allocated [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mregion `[0m[1;39m[[0m[1;36m0x515000000580[0m[39m,[0m[1;36m0x515000000775[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` of size [0m[1;36m501[0m[39m bytes.  [0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The buffer was allocated on the heap in `htmlSecureComment` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mvia the fuzzer’s [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`xmlFuzzMalloc` wrapper[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, not on the stack.  [0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The overrun occurs while processing an HTML comment, suggesting insufficient [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbounds checking on comment content length.  [0m                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The crash stack trace cycles through the HTML parser’s comment-handling routines:[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • htmlTopParseComment → htmlSecureComment → htmlParseDocument → [0m                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mhtmlCtxtParseDocument → LLVMFuzzerTestOneInput → Fuzzer driver.  [0m                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mAreas for Investigation  [0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- HTMLparser.c around the functions:  [0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • htmlSecureComment [0m[1;39m([0m[39mallocation size, length computations, buffer copies[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m  [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • htmlTopParseComment and htmlParseDocument [0m[1;39m([0m[39mhow comment length is determined and[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mpassed[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m  [0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The memory allocation wrapper `xmlFuzzMalloc` in `fuzz/fuzz.c` to understand its [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msizing strategy.  [0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The fuzzer harness in `fuzz/html.c` that invokes the parser with arbitrary inputs[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mto confirm no preliminary truncation or sanity checks are performed.  [0m              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Any associated dict-driven logic [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`html.dict`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m that might influence parsing paths[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mleading to oversized copy operations.[0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Fix Strategy[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<fix_strategy>[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mTo eliminate the heap‐buffer‐overflow in htmlSecureComment without touching the [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfuzzer harness or wider library behavior, we must stop aliasing the parser’s tiny [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mspaceTab buffer for comment accumulation and instead give htmlSecureComment its own[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mindependent buffer—just as xmlParseComment already does. This change isolates [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcomment data, preserves existing reallocation logic, and prevents any out‐of‐bounds[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mwrites into ctxt->spaceTab.[0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. In HTMLparser.c, locate htmlSecureComment around the current lines [0m[1;36m3330[0m[39m–[0m[1;36m3336[0m[39m. [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mYou will see:[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      used = [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m;[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      buffer_size = ctxt->spaceMax;[0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      buffer = [0m[1;39m([0m[39mxmlChar *[0m[1;39m)[0m[39mctxt->spaceTab;[0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mbuffer == NULL[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          buffer_size = [0m[1;36m500[0m[39m;[0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          buffer = [0m[1;35mxmlMalloc[0m[1;39m([0m[39mbuffer_size + [0m[1;36m1[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          …  [0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   Replace that entire block with an independent allocation modeled on [0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mxmlParseComment:[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      [0m[35m/[0m[39m* Start fresh: own buffer for comment content *[0m[35m/[0m                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      size_t used = [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m;[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      size_t buffer_size = XML_PARSER_BUFFER_SIZE;     [0m[35m/[0m[39m* typically [0m[1;36m500[0m[39m or defined [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mconstant *[0m[35m/[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      xmlChar *buffer = [0m[1;39m([0m[39mxmlChar *[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;35mxmlMalloc[0m[1;39m([0m[39mbuffer_size + [0m[1;36m1[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mbuffer == NULL[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          [0m[1;35mhtmlErrMemory[0m[1;39m([0m[39mctxt[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          goto error;[0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. Remove all references to ctxt->spaceTab and ctxt->spaceMax in htmlSecureComment:[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   – Do not seed buffer from ctxt->spaceTab.[0m                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   – Do not ever xmlRealloc on ctxt->spaceTab; always realloc your local buffer [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mpointer.[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   – Leave subsequent “if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mextraSize > buffer_size[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m… [0m[1;35mxmlRealloc[0m[1;39m([0m[39mbuffer, …[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m” logic [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39muntouched.[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. Ensure the rest of htmlSecureComment still frees its local buffer on exit [0m[1;39m([0m[39min [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthe existing error or return paths[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, so there are no leaks:[0m                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      error:[0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mbuffer[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;35mxmlFree[0m[1;39m([0m[39mbuffer[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. Include or verify the header where XML_PARSER_BUFFER_SIZE is defined [0m[1;39m([0m[39me.g., [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mparser.h or parserInternals.c[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m so the compiler knows the initial allocation size.[0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. Compile and rerun AddressSanitizer and libFuzzer:[0m                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   – The buffer now starts large enough [0m[1;39m([0m[39mXML_PARSER_BUFFER_SIZE bytes[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m and only [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mgrows via xmlRealloc, eliminating the write‐past‐end.[0m                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   – ctxt->spaceTab remains dedicated to the parser’s internal space stack and is [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mno longer corrupted.[0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mRationale[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m=========[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m– Core Insight: htmlSecureComment was incorrectly reusing ctxt->spaceTab [0m[1;39m([0m[39msize [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39munder fuzzing[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m as the comment buffer, triggering realloc mis‐management and [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39multimately an overflow.[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m– By giving htmlSecureComment its own buffer identical to xmlParseComment’s [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mstrategy, we preserve all existing copying and reallocation logic, satisfy the same[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfuzz harness, and avoid altering harness or test code.[0m                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m– This patch addresses the root cause [0m[1;39m([0m[39mmisuse of spaceTab[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, fully prevents the [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39moverflow, and has minimal impact on unrelated parser behavior.[0m                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m– Potential side effect is a small increase in memory for comments, but this [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mmatches how text nodes are normally handled and is negligible for typical HTML [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mparsing.[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mfix_strategy[0m[1m>[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ===Evaluation [33mEnd[0m===                                                                [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode_snippets[0m[39m>[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Fix Strategy[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<fix_strategy>[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. Revert the incorrect use of the undefined `XML_PARSER_BUFFER_SIZE` macro.  [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mRemove the freshly‐added code at the top of `htmlSecureComment` that attempted to [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mallocate using that identifier.[0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. Restore the original pattern of reading `ctxt->spaceTab`[0m[35m/[0m[39m`ctxt->spaceMax` for [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthe scratch buffer, and only when `spaceTab == NULL`, allocate a new buffer. [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mReplace the hard‐coded fallback size `[0m[1;36m500[0m[39m` with the correctly defined HTML parser [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mconstant `HTML_PARSER_BIG_BUFFER_SIZE` [0m[1;39m([0m[1;36m1000[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m to match this file’s conventions.[0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. [0m[1;39m([0m[39mOptional enhancement[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m Honor the `maxLength` parameter passed from [0m              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`htmlTopParseComment`.  Compute the initial allocation size as:[0m                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     initial_size = [0m[1;35mMIN[0m[1;39m([0m[39m [0m[1;39m([0m[39msize_t[0m[1;39m)[0m[39mmaxLength, HTML_PARSER_BIG_BUFFER_SIZE [0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   if `maxLength > [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m`, otherwise fall back to `HTML_PARSER_BIG_BUFFER_SIZE`.  This [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mensures that if the parser was invoked with `HTML_PARSE_HUGE`, the buffer can grow [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mto at least `XML_MAX_HUGE_LENGTH` later via the existing resize logic, but starts [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mlarge enough to avoid repeated reallocations for typical comment lengths.[0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. Update the fallback branch in `htmlSecureComment` accordingly:[0m                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   ```c[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   used = [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m;[0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   buffer_size = ctxt->spaceMax;[0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   buffer = [0m[1;39m([0m[39mxmlChar *[0m[1;39m)[0m[39mctxt->spaceTab;[0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mbuffer == NULL[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       size_t initial = HTML_PARSER_BIG_BUFFER_SIZE;[0m                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mmaxLength > [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m && [0m[1;39m([0m[39msize_t[0m[1;39m)[0m[39mmaxLength < initial[0m[1;39m)[0m                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m           initial = [0m[1;39m([0m[39msize_t[0m[1;39m)[0m[39mmaxLength;[0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       buffer = [0m[1;39m([0m[39mxmlChar *[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;35mxmlMalloc[0m[1;39m([0m[39minitial + [0m[1;36m1[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mbuffer == NULL[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m           [0m[1;35mhtmlErrMemory[0m[1;39m([0m[39mctxt[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m           return NULL;        [0m[35m/[0m[39m* no undefined macro, direct return *[0m[35m/[0m              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       buffer_size = initial;[0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   ```[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. Leave the downstream reallocation logic and the final saving of `buffer` into [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`ctxt->spaceTab`[0m[35m/[0m[39m`ctxt->spaceMax` unchanged.  This preserves the doubling‐capacity [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mstrategy on overflow and reuses the allocated buffer on subsequent calls.[0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m6[0m[39m. Do not introduce or modify any fuzz harness or test code.  No changes to [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mexternal utilities or headers beyond using the existing [0m                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`HTML_PARSER_BIG_BUFFER_SIZE` define in `HTMLparser.c`.[0m                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mJustification:[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- By using `HTML_PARSER_BIG_BUFFER_SIZE` [0m[1;39m([0m[1;36m1000[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m instead of the undefined [0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`XML_PARSER_BUFFER_SIZE`, compilation errors are eliminated.[0m                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- A larger initial buffer avoids the original [0m[1;36m500[0m[39m‐byte overflow, while the existing[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mgrowth logic [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`xmlRealloc`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m handles comments longer than [0m[1;36m1000[0m[39m bytes.[0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The optional use of `maxLength` respects the parser’s “huge” mode, without [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mintroducing new macros or breaking backward compatibility.[0m                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Existing SAX callbacks and memory‐free paths remain unchanged, ensuring no harm [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mto current functionality or test suites.[0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- No harness or utility code is touched, conforming to the requirement that only [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthe core parser logic be modified.[0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mPotential side‐effects & mitigation:[0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Increasing the fallback buffer from [0m[1;36m500[0m[39m to [0m[1;36m1000[0m[39m bytes slightly raises memory use [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mper parser context, but this is modest and offset by fewer realloc calls.[0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- If a comment exceeds [0m[1;36m1000[0m[39m bytes, the doubling logic will still safely reallocate;[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthere is no regression in handling very long comments.[0m                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The C23 “label followed by declaration” warning elsewhere in the function is [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbenign; it can be suppressed or cleaned later if desired, but does not prevent [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcompilation.[0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcode_range:[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mHTMLparser.[0m[1;92mc:3317[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m3336[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mHTMLparser.[0m[1;92mc:3577[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m3587[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mfix_strategy[0m[1m>[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ===Evaluation [33mEnd[0m===                                                                [2m                [0m
